            var googletag = googletag || {};
                googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

                    googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();

            pbjs.que.push(function() {
                pbjs.addAdUnits(adUnits);
                pbjs.requestBids({
                    bidsBackHandler: sendAdserverRequest
                });

            function sendAdserverRequest() {
                if (pbjs.adserverRequestSent) return;
                pbjs.adserverRequestSent = true;
                googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                    pbjs.que.push(function() {
                        pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();

                        var targetingParams = pbjs.getAdserverTargeting();
                        //console.log(JSON.stringify(targetingParams, null, 2));
                    });
                });
            }

            setTimeout(function() {
                sendAdserverRequest();
            }, PREBID_TIMEOUT);
        </script>

            $( document ).ready(function() {
                // GTM Session Set
                var maxExpire = new Date('2038-01-19 00:00:00');
                if (Cookies.get("gtm_session_first") === undefined) {
                    Cookies.set("gtm_session_first", new Date(), {expires: maxExpire})
                }            

                Cookies.set("gtm_session_last", new Date(), {expires: maxExpire})
                
                // ICO Banner Prefs
                var wrapper = $('#enjin-header');
                
                if (Cookies.get("icobanner_noshow13") != "1") {
                    $('#enjin-header').show();
                }

                $(".icobanner-close").on('click', function () {
                    Cookies.set("icobanner_noshow13", "1", {expires: 1})
                    wrapper.fadeOut();
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'customEvent',
                        'eventCategory': 'Countdown Banner',
                        'eventAction': 'Close',
                        'eventLabel': 'enjincoin',
                    });
                });
                
            });
